# Function Call Graph — Master List v1.6.29

Source: `Master_List/Current Production Script/v.1.6.29_Current_Production_Script`.

Scope: generated from all named function declarations in the production script. Calls are limited to calls from one in-script named function to another in-script named function, including named callback references passed to common Array methods. Google Apps Script services, JavaScript built-ins, object methods, anonymous callbacks, and menu string registrations are excluded unless they call or reference a named in-script function inside the function body.

Function count: 682. Edge count: 1744.

Legend: each row presents `Parent ↓ Child ↓ Grandchild`. Child rows have call depth `1`; grandchild rows have call depth `2`. `Recursive` is `Yes` when the parent can reach itself through direct or indirect calls.
